 The moon is coming close to the Earth and will be seen on Saturday night
 is dauraan chandramaa 18 saal main pehali baar dharti se apni saamaanya duuri kii tulana main 30,000 mile kareeb aa jayega
 This new form of the moon is being called a 'supermoon'
 yah supermun vibhinn jagahon par alag-alag samay par dekha ja sakegaa
 Local time in London 6
 15 baje se 6
 The moon will be seen between 45 o'clock
 dharti se apni saamaanya duuri kii tulana main 30,000 kilometre nikat hone ke kaaran iskaa aakaar tulanaatmak rup se bada dikhaai degaa haalanki shaam ko roshni zyada hone par ise dekhne main mushkil ho sakati he
 Actually, the size of the moon does not increase or decrease, but it appears smaller and larger when it is far and near the earth
 holi se pehle chand kii is diwaali ke myne aakhir kya hai or insaanon or dharti par iskaa kya asar padegaa is vishay par in dinon se kaaphi maathapai ho rahi he
 Eminent pundits and astrologers say that the impact of this moon coming close to the Earth has caused earthquakes in Japan and New Zealand and it will have more impact on the Earth during the state of supermoon
 iske kaaran agle do dinon main samudr main jowarbhata aa saktaa he
 Scientists already believe that it is due to the Moon's gravity that the waves in the sea become more high and tidal waves come
 duusari ore vaigyanik is baat se inkaar kar chuke hai ki supermun ke kisi asar ke kaaran japan main bhucamp aayaa or tsunami lehren uthin
 Scientists say that the earth's crust continuously adjusts itself to pressure, so earthquakes occur from time to time, the moon has no effect on them

" ' Auto exporters are facing difficulties in doing business due to GST

 Due to this, their working capital has increased considerably
 auto niryaatkon ke kaarobaar par jiesti kaa asar isi se saaf najar aata he ki july se oktober ke bich paisanger whical kaa niryaat 14
 45 percent reduction
